Objective: Analyze cardiovascular risk trends based on cholesterol values over 15 years, identifying periods of concern and calculating key risk ratios including Total/HDL ratio and non-HDL cholesterol trends

Need to assess cardiovascular risk patterns, identify concerning trends, and evaluate whether values fall within healthy ranges per current ACC/AHA guidelines.

Expected Output: 1) Trend analysis showing direction and rate of change for each cholesterol metric; 2) Calculation of Total/HDL ratio trends when data available; 3) Identification of periods where multiple markers moved in concerning directions; 4) Assessment of values against healthy range guidelines (LDL <100, HDL >40 men/>50 women, Triglycerides <150); 5) Highlight any sustained periods of elevated cardiovascular risk

### 1. **Trend Analysis by Cholesterol Metric**

**LDL Cholesterol (Target <100 mg/dL):**
- 2013-2015: Started very low (38-84 mg/dL) 
- 2018-2019: Peaked at concerning levels (96-114 mg/dL) - **ABOVE TARGET**
- 2021-2022: Improved significantly (54-122 mg/dL, mostly <100)
- Overall trend: U-shaped curve with concerning elevation 2018-2019

**HDL Cholesterol (Target >40 mg/dL for men):**
- 2014: Critically low at 25 mg/dL - **HIGH RISK**
- 2015-2020: Persistently below target (33-39 mg/dL) - **SUBOPTIMAL**
- 2021-2022: Slight improvement (38-47 mg/dL), mostly at or above target
- Overall trend: Gradual improvement but historically concerning

**Triglycerides (Target <150 mg/dL):**
- 2013-2014: Severely elevated (179-426 mg/dL) - **VERY HIGH RISK**
- 2015: Still elevated (210 mg/dL)
- 2016-2019: Variable but often elevated (116-188 mg/dL)
- 2020-2023: Excellent control (51-95 mg/dL)
- 2025: Borderline elevation at 153 mg/dL - **REQUIRES MONITORING**

### 2. **Total/HDL Ratio Analysis (Target <5.0)**

The Total/HDL ratio showed concerning patterns:
- 2014: 5.64 - **HIGH RISK**
- 2018: Peak at 5.32 - **HIGH RISK**
- 2019: 4.5-4.72 - Elevated
- 2021-2022: Improved to 2.52-3.96 - **OPTIMAL**

### 3. **Non-HDL Cholesterol Trends**

- 2014-2015: 116-126 mg/dL
- 2018-2019: 126-147 mg/dL - **ELEVATED**
- 2021-2022: 67-139 mg/dL (improving trend)

### 4. **Periods of Highest Cardiovascular Risk**

**Critical Risk Period 1 (2013-2015):**
- Triglycerides: 179-426 mg/dL (extremely elevated)
- HDL: 25-33 mg/dL (critically low)
- Total/HDL ratio: 4.82-5.64 (high risk)
- **Multiple red flags indicating severe dyslipidemia**

**Critical Risk Period 2 (2018-2019):**

- HDL: 34-36 mg/dL (below target)
- Triglycerides: 115-188 mg/dL (often elevated)
- Total/HDL ratio: 4.5-5.32 (high risk)
- **Atherogenic lipid profile with multiple risk factors**

### 5. **Current Status and Recommendations**
